 (* Write a function to find the maximum difference between available pairs in the given tuple list. *)
let max_diff =
  let rec max_diff_helper (tuples, diff) =
    match tuples with
    | [] -> diff
    | (_, _) ->
      let (a, b) = tuples in
      let diff_a = max_diff_helper (tuples - [a], diff) in
      let diff_b = max_diff_helper (tuples - [b], diff) in
      if diff_a > diff_b then diff_a else diff_b
  in
  max_diff_helper (List.map (fun (a, b) -> (a, b)) tuples, 0)

    match tuples with
    | [] -> diff
    | (_, _) ->
      let (a, b) = tuples in
      let diff_a = max_diff_helper (tuples - [a], diff) in
      let diff_b = max_diff_helper (tuples - [b], diff) in
      if diff_a > diff_b then diff_a else diff_b
  in
  max_diff_helper (List.map (fun (a, b) -> (a, b)) tuples, 0)

 (* Write a function to find the maximum difference between available pairs in the given tuple list. *)
let max_diff =
  let rec max_diff_helper (tuples, diff) =
    match tuples with
    | [] -> diff
    | (_, _) ->
      let (a, b) = tuples in
      let diff_a = max_diff_helper (tuples - [a], diff) in
      let diff_b = max_diff_helper (tuples - [b], diff) in
      if diff_a > diff_b then diff_a else diff_b
  in
  max_diff_helper (List.map (fun (a, b) -> (a, b)) tuples, 0)

let max_diff =
  let rec max_diff_helper (tuples, diff) =
    match tuples with
    | [] -> diff
    | (_, _) ->
      let (a, b) = tuples in
      let diff_a = max_diff_helper (tuples - [a], diff) in
      let diff_b = max_diff_helper (tuples - [b], diff) in
      if diff_a > diff_b then diff_a else diff_b
  in
  max_diff_helper (List.map (fun (a, b) -> (a, b)) tuples, 0)
[@ocaml.test]
let test_max_diff () =
  let tuples =
    [
      (1, 2);
      (1, 3);
      (2, 3);
      (2, 4);
      (3, 4);
      (4, 5);
      (5, 6);
      (6, 7);
      (7, 8);
      (8, 9);
      (9, 10);
    ] in
  let diff = max_diff tuples in
  assert (diff = 6);
  ()
[@ocaml.test]
let test_max_diff_empty () =
  let tuples

 (* Write a function to find the maximum difference between available pairs in the given tuple list. *)
let max_diff =
  let rec max_diff_helper (tuples, diff) =
    match tuples with
    | [] -> diff
    | (_, _) ->
      let (a, b) = tuples in
      let diff_a = max_diff_helper (tuples - [a], diff) in
      let diff_b = max_diff_helper (tuples - [b], diff) in
      if diff_a > diff_b then diff_a else diff_b
  in
  max_diff_helper (List.map (fun (a, b) -> (a, b)) tuples, 0)

 (* Write a function to find the maximum difference between available pairs in the given tuple list. *)
let max_diff =
  let rec max_diff_helper (tuples, diff) =
    match tuples with
    | [] -> diff
    | (_, _) ->
      let (a, b) = tuples in
      let diff_a = max_diff_helper (tuples - [a], diff) in
      let diff_b = max_diff_helper (tuples - [b], diff) in
      if diff_a > diff_b then diff_a else diff_b
  in
  max_diff_helper (List.map (fun (a, b) -> (a, b)) tuples, 0)
[@ocaml.test]
let test_max_diff () =
  let tuples =
    [
      (1, 2);
      (1, 3);
      (2, 3);
      (2, 4);
      (3, 4);
      (4, 5);
      (5, 6);
      (6, 7);
      (7, 8);
      (8, 9);
      (9, 10);
    ] in
  let diff = max_diff tuples in
  assert (diff = 6);
  ()
[@ocaml.test]
let test_max_diff_empty () =
  let tuples = [] in
  let diff = max_diff tuples in
  assert (diff = 0);
  ()
[@ocaml.test]

 (* Write a function to find the maximum difference between available pairs in the given tuple list. *)
let max_diff =
  let rec max_diff_helper (tuples, diff) =
    match tuples with
    | [] -> diff
    | (_, _) ->
      let (a, b) = tuples in
      let diff_a = max_diff_helper (tuples - [a], diff) in
      let diff_b = max_diff_helper (tuples - [b], diff) in
      if diff_a > diff_b then diff_a else diff_b
  in
  max_diff_helper (List.map (fun (a, b) -> (a, b)) tuples, 0)
[@ocaml.test]
let test_max_diff () =
  let tuples =
    [
      (1, 2);
      (1, 3);
      (2, 3);
      (2, 4);
      (3, 4);
      (4, 5);
      (5, 6);
      (6, 7);
      (7, 8);
      (8, 9);
      (9, 10);
    ] in
  let diff = max_diff tuples in
  assert (diff = 6);
  ()
[@ocaml.test]

  let tuples = [] in
  let diff = max_diff tuples in
  assert (diff = 0);

 (* Write a function to find the maximum difference between available pairs in the given tuple list. *)
let max_diff =
  let rec max_diff_helper (tuples, diff) =
    match tuples with
    | [] -> diff
    | (_, _) ->
      let (a, b) = tuples in
      let diff_a = max_diff_helper (tuples - [a], diff) in

  in

 (* Write a function to find the maximum difference between available pairs in the given tuple list. *)
let max_diff =
  let rec max_diff_helper (tuples, diff) =
    match tuples with
    | [] -> diff
    | (_, _) ->
      let (a, b) = tuples in
      let diff_a = max_diff_helper (tuples - [a], diff) in
      let diff_b = max_diff_helper (tuples - [b], diff) in
      if diff_a > diff_b then diff_a else diff_b
  in

 (* Write a function to find the maximum difference between available pairs in the given tuple list. *)
let max_diff =
  let rec max_diff_helper (tuples, diff) =
    match tuples with
    | [] -> diff
    | (_, _) ->
      let (a, b) = tuples in
      let diff_a = max_diff_helper (tuples - [a], diff) in
      let diff_b = max_diff_helper (tuples - [b], diff) in
      if diff_a > diff_b then diff_a else diff_b
  in
  max_diff_helper (List.map (fun (a, b) -> (a, b)) tuples, 0)

 (* Write a function to find the maximum difference between available pairs in the given tuple list. *)
let max_diff =
  let rec max_diff_helper (tuples, diff) =
    match tuples with
    | [] -> diff
    | (_, _) ->
      let (a, b) = tuples in
      let diff_a = max_diff_helper (tuples - [a], diff) in
      let diff_b = max_diff_helper (tuples - [b], diff) in
      if diff_a > diff_b then diff_a else diff_b
  in
  max_diff_helper (List.map (fun (a, b) -> (a, b)) tuples, 0)

 (* Write a function to find the maximum difference between available pairs in the given tuple list. *)
let max_diff =
  let rec max_diff_helper (tuples, diff) =
    match tuples with
    | [] -> diff
    | (_, _) ->
      let (a, b) = tuples in
      let diff_a = max_diff_helper (tuples - [a], diff) in
      let diff_b = max_diff_helper (tuples - [b], diff) in

  in

 (* Write a function to find the maximum difference between available pairs in the given tuple list. *)
let max_diff =
  let rec max_diff_helper (tuples, diff) =
    match tuples with
    | [] -> diff
    | (_, _) ->
      let (a, b) = tuples in
      let diff_a = max_diff_helper (tuples - [a], diff) in
      let diff_b = max_diff_helper (tuples - [b], diff) in
      if diff_a > diff_b then diff_a else diff_b
  in
  max_diff_helper (List.map (fun (a, b) -> (a, b)) tuples, 0)

 (* Write a function to find the maximum difference between available pairs in the given tuple list. *)
let max_diff =
  let rec max_diff_helper (tuples, diff) =
    match tuples with
    | [] -> diff
    | (_, _) ->
      let (a, b) = tuples in
      let diff_a = max_diff_helper (tuples - [a], diff) in
      let diff_b = max_diff_helper (tuples - [b], diff) in
      if diff_a > diff_b then diff_a else diff_b
  in
  max_diff_helper (List.map (fun (a, b) -> (a, b)) tuples, 0)

 (* Write a function to find the maximum difference between available pairs in the given tuple list. *)
let max_diff =
  let rec max_diff_helper (tuples, diff) =
    match tuples with
    | [] -> diff
    | (_, _) ->
      let (a, b) = tuples in
      let diff_a = max_diff_helper (tuples - [a], diff) in
      let diff_b = max_diff_helper (tuples - [b], diff) in
      if diff_a > diff_b then diff_a else diff_b
  in
  max_diff_helper (List.map (fun (a, b) -> (a, b)) tuples, 0)

      (6, 7);

      (9, 10);
    ] in
  let diff = max_diff tuples in
  assert (diff = 6);

 (* Write a function to find the maximum difference between available pairs in the given tuple list. *)
let max_diff =
  let rec max_diff_helper (tuples, diff) =
    match tuples with
    | [] -> diff
    | (_, _) ->
      let (a, b) = tuples in
      let diff_a = max_diff_helper (tuples - [a], diff) in
      let diff_b = max_diff_helper (tuples - [b], diff) in
      if diff_a > diff_b then diff_a else diff_b
  in
  max_diff_helper (List.map (fun (a, b) -> (a, b)) tuples, 0)
[@ocaml.test]
let test_max_diff () =
  let tuples =
    [
      (1, 2);
      (1, 3);
      (2, 3);
      (2, 4);
      (3, 4);
      (4, 5);
      (5, 6);
      (6, 7);
      (7, 8);
      (8, 9);
      (9, 10);
    ] in
  let diff = max_diff tuples in
  assert (diff = 6);
  ()
[@ocaml.test]
let test_max_diff_empty () =
  let tuples = [] in
  let diff = max_diff tuples in
  assert (diff = 0);
  ()
[@ocaml.test]
let test_max_diff_singleton () =
  let tuples =
    [
      (1, 2);
    ] in
  let diff = max_diff tuples in
  assert (diff = 1);
  ()

    ] in
  let diff = max_diff tuples in
  assert (diff = 0);

 (* Write a function to find the maximum difference between available pairs in the given tuple list. *)
let max_diff =
  let rec max_diff_helper (tuples, diff) =
    match tuples with
    | [] -> diff
    | (_, _) ->
      let (a, b) = tuples in
      let diff_a = max_diff_helper (tuples - [a], diff) in
      let diff_b = max_diff_helper (tuples - [b], diff) in
      if diff_a > diff_b then diff_a else diff_b
  in
  max_diff_helper (List.map (fun (a, b) -> (a, b)) tuples, 0)

    match tuples with
    | [] -> diff
    | (_, _) ->
      let (a, b) = tuples in
      let diff_a = max_diff_helper (tuples - [a], diff) in
      let diff_b = max_diff_helper (tuples - [b], diff) in
      if diff_a > diff_b then diff_a else diff_b
  in
  max_diff_helper (List.map (fun (a, b) -> (a, b)) tuples, 0)
[@ocaml.test]
let test_max_diff () =
  let tuples =
    [
      (1, 2);
      (1, 3);
      (2, 3);
      (2, 4);
      (3, 4);
      (4, 5);
      (5, 6);
      (6, 7);
      (7, 8);
      (8, 9);
      (9, 10);
    ] in
  let diff = max_diff tuples in
  assert (diff = 6);
  ()
[@ocaml.test]
let test_max_diff_empty () =
  let tuples = [] in
  let diff = max_diff tuples in
  assert (diff = 0);
  ()

  let tuples =

      (1, 2);
    ] in

  assert (diff = 1);

 (* Write a function to find the maximum difference between available pairs in the given tuple list. *)
let max_diff =
  let rec max_diff_helper (tuples, diff) =
    match tuples with
    | [] -> diff
    | (_, _) ->
      let (a, b) = tuples in
      let diff_a = max_diff_helper (tuples - [a], diff) in
      let diff_b = max_diff_helper (tuples - [b], diff) in
      if diff_a > diff_b then diff_a else diff_b
  in
  max_diff_helper (List.map (fun (a, b) -> (a, b)) tuples, 0)
